<script>
  var baseURL = "https://gamepress.gg";

  function enableDM() {
    var newNode = {
      _links: {
          type: {
              href: baseURL + '/user/{user}'
          }
      },
      field_dark_mode: {
          value: 1
      }
    };
    getCsrfToken(function(csrfToken) {
        postNode(csrfToken, newNode);
    });
  }

  function getCsrfToken(callback) {
    jQuery
      .get(Drupal.url('session/token'))
      .done(function (data) {
        var csrfToken = data;
        callback(csrfToken);
      });
  }

  function patchNode(csrfToken, node) {
  var urlJSON = baseURL + '/user/' + userID2 + '?_format=hal_json'
  jQuery.ajax({
    url: urlJSON,
    method: 'PATCH',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/hal+json',
      'X-CSRF-Token': csrfToken
    },
    data: JSON.stringify(node),
    success: function (node) {
      window.location.href = baseURL;
    }
  });
}

function decodeHtml(html) {
    var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
    txt.innerHTML = html;
    return txt.value;
}

function getPathByValue(value){
    for(var i = 0; i < list.length; i++){
        if(list[i].toLowerCase() == value.toLowerCase()){
            return paths[i];
        }
    }
}
/* Set the width of the side navigation to 250px */

function openNav() {
  var $slider = document.getElementById('sidenav');
  $slider.setAttribute("class", "slide-in");
  document.getElementById("overlay").style.display = "block";
  document.getElementById("menu-close").style.display = "block";
  document.getElementById("bottom-sticky-ad").style.display = "none";
  document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
}

function closeNav() {
  var $slider = document.getElementById('sidenav');
  $slider.setAttribute("class", "slide-out");
  document.getElementById("overlay").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("menu-close").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("bottom-sticky-ad").style.display = "block";
  document.body.style.overflow = "auto";
}

</script>

<h2><a href="/grandorder/item/crystallized-lore" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Crystallized Lore</span>
</a></h2>
<div class="field field--name-field-item-icon field--type-image field--label-hidden field__item"> <a href="/grandorder/item/crystallized-lore" hreflang="en"><img src="/grandorder/sites/grandorder/files/styles/height50px/public/2017-10/Crystallized_lore_0.png?itok=s866dPqy" width="46" height="50" alt="" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-height50px" />

<script>
      let ascensionTotals = [];
      let skillTotals = [];
      let totalTotals = [];
      let appendTotals = [];
      let totalTotalTotals = []; //lol
      let totalQP = 0;
      let totalTotalTotalQP = 0;
      let totalQPAsc = 0;
      let totalQPSkill = 0;
      let totalQPAppend = 0;
      const matsHelper = (className, counterArray, multiplier) => {
        $("." + className + " .paragraph--type--required-materials").each(function(){
          const item = $(this).data("item");
          const qty = parseInt($(this).data("qty")) * multiplier;
          if(counterArray[item]){
            //just add to the existing counter
            counterArray[item]["qty"] = counterArray[item]["qty"] + parseInt(qty);
          }
          else{
            //add to the existing counter and also store the html to output
            counterArray[item] = {};
            counterArray[item]["html"] = $(this)[0].innerHTML;
            counterArray[item]["qty"] = parseInt(qty);
          }
        });
      }
      const sumTotals = (totals) => {
        const toReturn = {};
        for(const total of totals){
          for(const item in total){
            if(toReturn[item]){
              toReturn[item].qty += total[item].qty;
            }
            else{
              toReturn[item] = {};
              toReturn[item].html = total[item].html;
              toReturn[item].qty = total[item].qty;
            }
          }
        }
        return toReturn;
      }
      const printTotalMats = (element, totalArray) => {
        for(key in totalArray){
          var currItemDiv = document.createElement("div");
          currItemDiv.className = "paragraph--type--required-materials";
          currItemDiv.innerHTML = totalArray[key]["html"];
          element.appendChild(currItemDiv);
          $(currItemDiv).find(".field--name-field-number-of-materials").html("x" + totalArray[key]["qty"]);
        }
      }
      $(document).ready(function(){
        //summing total QP
        $(".ascension-cost div").each(function(){
          totalQPAsc += parseInt($(this).attr("content"));
        });
        $("#Skill-materials-table .Skill-cost").each(function(){
          totalQPSkill += parseInt($(this).html().replace(/,/g, ""));
        });
        $("#append-Skill-materials-table .Skill-cost").each(function(){
          totalQPAppend += parseInt($(this).html().replace(/,/g, ""));
        });
        totalQPSkill *= 3;
        totalQPAppend *= 3;
        totalQP = totalQPAsc + totalQPSkill;
        totalTotalTotalQP = totalQP + totalQPAppend;
        matsHelper("ascension-materials", ascensionTotals, 1, totalTotals);
        matsHelper("Skill-materials", skillTotals, 3, totalTotals);
        matsHelper("append-Skill-materials", appendTotals, 3);

        totalTotals = sumTotals([ascensionTotals, skillTotals]);
        totalTotalTotals = sumTotals([totalTotals, appendTotals]); 

        const ascensionEle = document.getElementById("ascension-total");
        printTotalMats(ascensionEle, ascensionTotals);
        createQPDiv(ascensionEle, totalQPAsc);

        const skillEle = document.getElementById("skill-total");
        printTotalMats(skillEle, skillTotals);
        createQPDiv(skillEle, totalQPSkill);

        const totalEle = document.getElementById("total-total");
        printTotalMats(totalEle, totalTotals);
        createQPDiv(totalEle, totalQP);

        const appendEle = document.getElementById("append-total");
        if(appendEle){
          printTotalMats(appendEle, appendTotals);
          createQPDiv(appendEle, totalQPAppend);

          const totalTotalTotalsEle = document.getElementById("total-total-total");
          printTotalMats(totalTotalTotalsEle, totalTotalTotals)
          createQPDiv(totalTotalTotalsEle, totalTotalTotalQP);
        }
        


      });

    function createQPDiv(container, qp){
      //  /sites/grandorder/files/2017-10/Qp.png
      var qpDiv = document.createElement("div");
      qpDiv.className = "total-qp-div clearfix";


      var qpImg = document.createElement("img");
      qpImg.src = "/sites/grandorder/files/2017-10/Qp.png";
      qpDiv.appendChild(qpImg);

      var amtDiv = document.createElement("div");
      amtDiv.className = "qp-amt";
      amtDiv.innerHTML = "x" + qp.toLocaleString();
      qpDiv.appendChild(amtDiv);

      container.appendChild(qpDiv);
    }
    </script>
<h2 class="main-title">Total Materials Required</h2>

<h2 class="main-title">Table of Contents</h2>
<ul class="servant-tabs">

</ul>
<h2 class="main-title">Overview</h2>
<p><span><span><span><span><em><span>Seeing happy, healthy people makes me want to vomit.</span></em></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>One day, Caren became bored with her job as an elementary school nurse since nobody came in half-dead, so she decided to kill people herself. As an </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>AoE Quick Ruler</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> she serves this role well to become one of the forefront loopers in the game.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Carens kit is surprisingly strong both for farming and in more challenging quests. In farming, she is an exceptional looper, being only one of the few capable of unleashing three Noble Phantasms in a row with two Skadis and any MC she desires. She is also the first Servant capable of Quick Looping with a Black Grail. Outside of looping in regards to farming, she has two on-demand self charges in </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Golden Arrow A </span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>and </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Mana Burst (Love) A</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>, as well as a three turn NP gauge leech, making her refund potential off the charts. She also carries extreme durability in the form of a three-hit three-turn invincibility on </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Shroud of Valentinus A</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> along with an innate Class resistance to all classes save Berserker and Extra classes. On top of that, she can even negate an entire enemy Noble Phantasm by using that skill. On top of </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><em><span>that</span></em></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>, she has a nullify buff effect on her Noble Phantasm which can erase some of the trickier buffs enemies get in Challenge Quests. </span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Her main shortfall is that while she is great at looping, she doesnt do much damage to go with it. As a result of her being a Ruler class and there very rarely being Moon Cancers in the game, she often stands as a tank as opposed to a machine gun. She also requires very specific setups to work at her best, making her much weaker for Masters without specific Servants. </span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Caren may hate children and confuse a stroke with dizziness, but she knows how to apply the hurt time and time again. Just dont ask her for a bandaid or shell give you the entire first aid kit!</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 class="main-title">Strengths</h2>
<div id="servant-strengths">
<h3><span><span><span><span><span><span>Looping</span></span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Carens 5-hit AoE Quick Noble Phantasm gives her decent refund on her Noble Phantasm. Having two self-charges and a 3-turn leech make it so that she can use her refund and two Skadis to release 3 Noble Phantasms with very few exceptions (assuming a Master has an MLB Kaleidoscope, or can start with another 50% charger to charge her up to 50%). Shes also the first Servant who can AoE Quick loop using a Black Grail.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3><span><span><span><span><span><span>Durable</span></span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Like all Rulers, Caren takes half damage against almost every enemy type. With her high HP base, shes tough to bring down as is. But when one considers her 3-hit 3-turn invincibility on a moderately short 6-turn cooldown, she becomes hard to touch without specific skills. And when one considers how she can both reduce incoming damage from enemies by 20% and has two NP drains, its going to be tough to knock her out.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3><span><span><span><span><span><span>Strong Support</span></span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>While Carens NP leech seems to be the exact opposite of support, shes actually a great support for the team capable of boosting their NP gain rates, lowering incoming damage, and taking a 1-turn taunt. Most notably, her Shroud of Valentinus gives an on-demand 1-hit Invincibility to the party, negating the effects of any unbuffed enemy Noble Phantasm which could arrive the next turn. Even better, she can trivialize a Challenge quest via her Noble Phantasms nullify block, which will have the enemies use their timed buffs but lose their effects (as opposed to a skill seal which simply delays them for a turn or two). </span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</div>
<h2 class="main-title">Weaknesses</h2>
<div id="servant-weaknesses">
<h3><span><span><span><span><span><span>Low Damage</span></span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Caren has very rare situations where she can utilise her class advantage against Moon Cancers (especially in an AoE setting), meaning she is almost always going to be dealing neutral damage. Her skills also do very little for her damage outside of a 20% Quick up and a passive to gain 20% attack up if she is debuffed. Most of her damage boost will come from supports and CEs.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3><span><span><span><span><span><span>High Bar of Entry</span></span></span></span></span></span></h3>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>For Caren to work at her best, Masters might need 112 points for their team to use 5 event CEs (which may be SSRs at 12 points a piece), 5 SSR Event CEs (60 points), 3 specific support SSR Servants (48 points), and Angra Mainyu (4 points). The SSR Servants which make her work, Skadi and Altria Caster, are highly limited as well. Without these requirements, she becomes mediocre in scope. </span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</div>

<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Carens skills carry a huge list of effects, but when it comes down to it, they consist of three charges working in different ways. Masters should prioritize skill levelling based on how to best charge her.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Shroud of Valentinus A</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> is an amazing skill which grants her invincibility for three hits over three turns, and the rest of the party one hit. Even better for her, it will leech 10% NP from every ally on the field for three turns, enabling her looping with lower refunds. Masters will want to use this skill either at the start when looping, or when the enemy is about to use a Noble Phantasm. The NP gain rate for allies in practice is near trivial, and the only thing which scales with leveling. Masters should raise this last because of this, although reaching level 10 is still ultimately desirable to get the 6-turn cooldown.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Golden Arrow A </span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>is the first of Carens two charges, which takes away 1 tick of charge from an enemy, while at the same time giving one to herself. This is a great skill for when multiple enemies are about to unleash Single Target Noble Phantasms, as it provides a 20% attack and defense down debuff on all enemies, and focuses all attacks onto Caren. With a 3-hit invincibility, this negates all enemy Noble Phantasms for the turn (or 2 of them, as 1 will be unable to NP due to the drain). As this skills charging is immediately relevant for looping, this skill should always be leveled first and to the max.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Mana Burst (Love) A</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> is the second of Carens two charge skills, taking away 1 tick of charge from an enemy. This is also her only steroid, providing a 20% Quick up which is for the most part trivial for looping and damage. While it gives 20% card up for Arts and Buster as well, these rarely make any difference. This should be leveled to max, and second as the extra Quick buff is less important than the attack decrease in Golden Arrow, and this skills NP charge ceiling is lower. </span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<td>
<h2 class="main-title">Craft Essence Recommendation</h2>
<div class="views-element-container"><div class="view view-craft-essence-recommendation view-id-craft_essence_recommendation view-display-id-block_1 js-view-dom-id-4f4682287e6fdd73fe22f5541762cad47460920b8791d51c75ef9ce06ec0f4c7">
<div class="view-content">
<table class="views-table views-view-table cols-0" id="sort-table">

</div>

</div>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>As Caren is applicable in both farming and challenge quests, Masters will want to use CEs for the situation. When farming, Masters will want to use a </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Starting NP Gauge </span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>CE, potentially with a </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Mixed Starting Gauge/Damage</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> effect to enable a 3-turn loop. In the case of using her against Casters, Masters may even want to consider </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>NP Damage Up</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> CEs to boost her damage. If using her in a challenge quest, Masters will still want to use her Noble Phantasm as often as possible via </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>NP Regen Per Turn</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> CEs.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Kaleidoscope / The Imaginary Element / Holy Night Supper / Knights of Marines / Golden Sumo: Boulder Tournament </span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>- Caren is a looper, making an MLB Kaleidoscope a must have. Without it, any CE which provides at least a 50% charge will work using a Plugsuit. The best ones are the ones which will increase her damage. NP Gain CEs such as Magical Girl of Sapphire are often wasted on her as she refunds enough without further NP Gain support.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>The Black Grail</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> - Using the Altria and double Skadi strategy against Casters and some Riders, Masters will want the largest boost possible to her Noble Phantasm damage.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Prisma Cosmos </span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span>- In a non-farming situation, Caren will want to use her Noble Phantasm as many times as possible to damage and debuff the enemy with Quick Downs. 10% a turn will add up to far more than a starting gauge in a longer fight. </span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<h2 class="main-title">Gameplay Tips</h2>
<p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Caren has two primary ways of looping aside from the traditional MLB KScope Skadi/Skadi and plugsuit Altria/Waver.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ol><li><span><span><span><span><span><span>Use two Skadis with at least 20% starting gauge. By popping Carens Shroud of Valentine, she will leech 10% from each of them per turn for 20% total. Added together with a 50% charge from Skadi and a 20% self-charge, she needs 10% total refund to loop (which is possible against almost all enemies).</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li><span><span><span><span><span><span>On most Caster waves and some Rider waves, Caren can run a Black Grail using Caster Altria and Two Skadis. Have the two Skadis on the front line, and use their Quick skills and one of their charges on her. Swap this Skadi out for Caster Altria, who provides the 30% AoE charge and 20% targetable of Caren. This will provide her leeching skill, and should refund 30% with both Quick buffs, and shell leech 20%. Use Carens charges turn 2 and Skadis charges turn 3 to complete the loop.</span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol><p><span><span><span><span><span><span>Carens Passive, </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Masochistic Spiritualistic Disposition EX</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> gives her a 20% attack bonus if she has a debuff on her. It is often wise to put </span></span></span></span></span></span><span><span><span><strong><span><span>Anra Mainiiu</span></span></strong></span></span></span><span><span><span><span><span><span> in the 5th slot of the team as his passive gives a debuff to all members of the team even when he is not on the field, so she can take advantage of her passive ATK buff. Note that her taunt does not count as a debuff.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
</div>

<h2 class="main-title">Profile</h2>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Character Info</h3>
<p>The god of love in Roman myth. A girl named Caren Hortensia was chosen for this Pseudo-Servant's vessel. The combination of Amor's Authority and Caren's personality melded so well together that they were reborn into the miraculous and perfectly fused Divine Spirit Caren! (Or so she claims.)</p>
<p>She was chosen to be a sacrifice as a Servant on humanity's side during the Incineration of Humanity. She may be a bit eccentric, but deep down it all stems from her devotion to this world!</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 1</h3>
<p>Height/Weight: 156cm, 40kg<br />
Origin: Greek mythology, Roman mythology, Fate/hollow ataraxia<br />
Region: Mediterranean Sea, Europe<br />
Alignment: Lawful-Good<br />
Gender: Female<br />
"No matter what form I take, I am a sister in service of the Lord, but I currently fulfill Amor's duties as well.<br />
You consider this conversion to a different faith?<br />
Worry not. The Lord is infinite in His love."</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 2</h3>
<p>In three words, Caren's personality can be described as dry, cool, and cynical. She may be a young girl, but you'll never hear her speak honeyed words. Is she a saintly devil, or a devilish saint?</p>
<p>Scathing. Clear-eyed. Abusive. Promiscuous. Ruthless. Caren has been described in these terms, but above all, she is a saint who is girlishly innocent at heart. Her powerful conviction and faith stem from her lifelong dedication to her Lord in Heaven and all the souls He loves.</p>
<p>When Caren was chosen to play Amor's role, the jolt that ran through her body was not revulsion toward a false god, but rather a thunderous sense of duty. Amor may be of a different pantheon, but his role as a messenger of love is an admirable one. Is not the best way to return God's love carrying out that duty with all her heart? And if that means unilaterally altering people's fates, who can blame her for being excited!? ...Burning with a newfound passion for her work, she changes her name to Caren C. Hortensia and sets off to bring righteousness to Valentine's Day at Chaldea.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 3</h3>
<p>Eros, the god of love in Greek mythology, and Amor, the god of love in Roman mythology, comprise Caren's divine core.</p>
<p>Although she goes by Amor in her angelic form, Caren uses her own name while in her default second Ascension form and completely rejects Eros (he's useless anyway). Furthermore, she puts impersonates Cupid, said to symbolize both of the aforementioned deities.</p>
<p>This behavior too stems from Caren's devout belief that love is selfless. Amor aside, this is also part of her rejection of Eros (sexual love).</p>
<p>In Greek philosophy, there are four types of love: erotic, friendly, philanthropic, and filial. Caren's idea of a god's philanthropic love (agape) shuns erotic love, which she sees as vulgar.</p>
<p>Thus, Caren is a Pseudo-Servant of Amor, a god of love, but fundamentally denies Amor and Eros, believing herself to be a messenger of a far greater form of love.</p>
<p>The eccentric, contradictory streak of masochism and sadism that runs through this Servant is indeed very much like Caren.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 4</h3>
<p>Item Construction: A<br />
A professional at fashioning tools to be used on the heart. This represents Caren's arrows of love. They'll give you a push when you're about to falter, stirring your heart to function even better. She can create many such wonderful items.</p>
<p>Independent Action: A<br />
Caren C. Hortensia, messenger of love, serves more than just her Master.<br />
She has a duty to the Lord's heart and to all the people His love must reach. She is not bound by her Master's business; she does whatever she wants.</p>
<p>Masochistic Medium's Nature: EX<br />
A physical disposition prone to being possessed by nearby demons, regardless of the owner's will. Recreates demons that exist as phenomena and, under certain conditions, physically incarnates them. Easily afflicted by Poison, Curse, and Burn-related status effects. Furthermore, Caren's offensive power increases while under such effects. Fearsome sadism born of masochism. Still, it's not something she can do on command.</p>
<p>Core of the Goddess: B<br />
This was originally Amor's Divinity skill, but his host's powerful faith has transformed it. To the girl, only her almighty Father possesses true divinity.</p>
<p>Iron Faith: A<br />
Caren's personal variant of the Craft Essence "Iron-Willed Training." An albino girl who should have died at birth defied all expectations and grew up. She believes that her survival can only be a miracle and physical proof of God's love. Acquired as a passive skill with resistance to Terror, Charm, and Buster effects.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 5</h3>
<p>[The Greatest Hits: "Calling Agape"]<br />
Rank: EX<br />
NP Type: Anti-Personnel<br />
Range: 1 - 99<br />
Maximum Targets: Unknown</p>
<p>Universally Unconditional and Infinite Love.<br />
This is a Noble Phantasm of heavenly ascent and descent as a prayer-cloaked agent of new, universal love. Caren transforms not into Amor, but the heavenly love at his source, delivering an attack of divine wrath that illuminates the world with unconditional and infinite love. Anyone can see that it's an anti-world Noble Phantasm, but its user insists that it's meant to be used against people. Caren's idea of love applies unconditionally to all of mankind. It is the purely selfless love of a god; it is agape.</p>
<p>Once upon a time, in tiger colosseum, Caren wielded a morning star named "My Weight Is Equal to My Wielder's Love." Caren loves all of humanity, ergo her hammer is as heavy as Earth, at least for the FGO edition.</p>
<p>The love beams are the infinite part, and it's unconditional because Caren generously won't charge you a fee for getting blasted.</p>
<p>Shroud of Valentinus: A<br />
Eros (erotic love). This was originally Caren's trusty Shroud of Magdala, but she's now using it as a "shroud of lovers." Apparently, she named it after Valentinus to play along with the holiday spirit at Chaldea.</p>
<p>Golden Arrow: A<br />
Philia (friendly love).<br />
Angelic arrows that Amorize human hearts they pierce. Forcefully.</p>
<p>"Love always comes as a surprise, doesn't it?"</p>
<p>Mana Burst (Love): A<br />
Storge (filial love) aka God Caren. A super-buff called forth for the singular one she loves and must protect. Sounds kinda awesome.</p>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--servant-profile-entry paragraph--view-mode--default">
<h3 class="sub-title" style="margin-top:8px">Profile 6</h3>
<p>Rather than Fate/hollow ataraxia...this is Caren from Fate/tiger colosseum. The girl dispatched as a Church Overseer was taciturn and spoke nothing of her own opinions and circumstances, but this time, freed from the duties of a sister, she's taken on the attitude of something more like a mastermind, freely talking, working, and scheming. (A mastermind she may be, but she's only working to create happiness for all, rather than acting out of any malice.)</p>
<p>...That said, Caren sure does have a troublesome personality, being as much of a masochist as she is a sadist. She loves seeing people suffer, and loves her own physical suffering. That's why she plans out better lives for people, but prepares harsh trials before any can reach those ends.</p>
<p>Caren approves of generating revenue, but only so she can use those funds as a symbol of authority or to control people. After all, people wish for God's love and dominion. To Caren, who occasionally becomes one with God's will during fervent prayer (according to her), earning money will lead to greater joy for all.</p>
<p>The Church teaches that it is wrong to hoard worldly wealth, but Caren does not consider money to be wealth, and cares little for the currency she gathers. She is simply excited by the act of accumulating money; she has no thoughts of buying nice things with that money, nor using it to live in luxury. It seems that to her, it is merely a resource to be spent.</p>
<p></p>
<p>While she has offered herself to any number of people and animals to exorcise their demons, thinking always of their happiness...she has only ever felt pure, human lovewishing someone else happiness for her own sakefor one person. Even now, the memories and wishes of that time are buried deep within her heart.</p>
</div>

<script>

function toggleBanners(id,element){
    var banners = document.getElementById(id);
    if(banners.style.display == "none"){
      banners.style.display = "";
    }
    else{
      banners.style.display = "none";
    }
  }


var servantHP, servantATK, servantHPG, servantATKG;
$(document).ready(function() {
  var currTime = new Date().getTime();
  $.getJSON("https://gamepress.gg/json-list?_format=json&game_tid=26&" + currTime, function(data) {
    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      var curr = data[i];
      if (data[i].title == "FGO Stat Rankings") {
        $.getJSON(curr.url, function(data) {
          servantHP = sortJSONByField(data, "hp");
          servantHPG = sortJSONByField(data, "grail_hp");
          servantATK = sortJSONByField(data, "atk");
          servantATKG = sortJSONByField(data, "grail_atk");
          setHPRank();
          setATKRank();
        })
      }
    }
  });
});

function setHPRank(){
  var hpText = document.getElementById("hpRank");
  var hp = "13,837"
  var gHP = "15,159"
  hp = hp.replace(",", "");
  gHP = gHP.replace(",", "");
  var data = getInfo(servantHP, "hp");
  var count = data[0];
  var highest = data[1];
  var width = parseInt(hp) / parseInt(highest);
  width = width * 100;
  document.getElementById("hp-bar").style.width = width + "%";

  var grailData = getInfo(servantHPG, "grail_hp");
  var grailHighest = grailData[1];
  var grailWidth = parseInt(gHP) / parseInt(grailHighest);
  grailWidth = grailWidth * 100;
  document.getElementById("hp-bar-max").style.width = grailWidth + "%";

  var hpRank = getRank(count, hp);
  hpText.innerHTML = "HP Rank: " + hpRank + "/" + servantHP.length;

}

function setATKRank(){
    var atkText = document.getElementById("atkRank");
  var atk = "11,351"
  var gatk = "12,425"
  atk = atk.replace(",", "");
  gatk = gatk.replace(",", "");
  var data = getInfo(servantATK, "atk");
  var count = data[0];
  var highest = data[1];
  var width = parseInt(atk) / parseInt(highest);
  width = width * 100;
  document.getElementById("atk-bar").style.width = width + "%";

  var grailData = getInfo(servantATKG, "grail_atk");
  var grailHighest = grailData[1];
  var grailWidth = parseInt(gatk) / parseInt(grailHighest);
  grailWidth = grailWidth * 100;
  document.getElementById("atk-bar-max").style.width = grailWidth + "%";

  var atkRank = getRank(count, atk);
  atkText.innerHTML = "ATK Rank: " + atkRank + "/" + servantATK.length;
}
  function getRank(array, stat){
    var rank = -1;
    var count = 0;
    for(var i = 0; i < array.length; i++){
      if(array[i] == stat){
        rank = i+1;
        return rank;
      }
    }
  }
  function getInfo(array, field){
    var uniques = [];
    var highest = -1;
    for(var i = 0; i < array.length; i++){
      var currVal = array[i][field];
      var currValInt = parseInt(currVal);
      var currClass = array[i].tdoll_class;
      if(currValInt > highest){
        highest = currValInt;
      }
      uniques.push(currVal);
    }
    return [uniques, highest];
  }

function sortJSONByField(json, field){
  return json.concat().sort(function(a, b){
    return parseInt(b[field]) - parseInt(a[field]);
  });
}
</script>
<script>
var nid = "939096";
$(document).ready(function() {
    $.getJSON('/grandorder/calc-stats?_format=json&nid=' + nid,
        function(data) {
            setGrowthChart(data);
        });
});

const ascensionProgressions = [
    [1, 20, 30, 40, 50, 60],
    [1, 25, 35, 45, 55, 65],
    [1, 30, 40, 50, 60, 70],
    [1, 40, 50, 60, 70, 80],
    [1, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90]
]

const grailProgressions = [
    [70, 75, 80, 85, 90, 92, 94, 96, 98, 100],
    [70, 75, 80, 85, 90, 92, 94, 96, 98, 100],
    [75, 80, 85, 90, 92, 94, 96, 98, 100],
    [85, 90, 92, 94, 96, 98, 100],
    [92, 94, 96, 98, 100]
]

const pointBackgroundColorsBlue = [
  ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black' ]
];
const pointBackgroundColorsBrown = [
  ['brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],

  ['brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
  ['brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'yellow', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black' ]
]

const capProgressions = [102, 104, 106, 108, 110, 112, 114, 116, 118, 120]
function setGrowthChart(data2) {
    var atks = [];
    var hps = [];
    var data = data2[0];

    var stars = "51";
    var rarity = 4;
    switch (stars) {
        case "51":
            rarity = 4;
            break;
        case "56":
            rarity = 3;
            break;
        case "61":
            rarity = 2;
            break;
        case "66":
            rarity = 1;
            break;
        case "71":
            rarity = 0;
            break;
        case "3046":
            rarity = 1;
            break;
    }

    var stars = parseInt("");
    var ascProg = ascensionProgressions[rarity];
    var grailProg = grailProgressions[rarity];
    var levels = ascProg.concat(grailProg);
    levels = levels.concat(capProgressions);
    for (var i = 0; i <= levels.length; i++) {
        var currLvl = levels[i];
        var curr = data["field_atk_" + currLvl];
        atks.push(curr);
        var currHP = data["field_hp_" + currLvl];
        hps.push(currHP);
    }

    var ctx = document.getElementById("growthChart");
    var hpsData = [];
    var atkData = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < levels.length; i++) {
        hpsData.push({
            x: levels[i],
            y: hps[i]
        });
        atkData.push({
            x: levels[i],
            y: atks[i]
        });
    }
    var config = {
        type: 'scatter',
        data: {
            datasets: [{
                    pointBackgroundColor: pointBackgroundColorsBlue[rarity],
                    pointBorderColor: ['blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'blue', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
                    label: 'HP',
                    data: hpsData,
                    borderColor: "blue",
                    backgroundColor: "blue",
                    fill: false
                },
                {
                    pointBackgroundColor: pointBackgroundColorsBrown[rarity],
                    pointBorderColor: ['brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'brown', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black', 'black'],
                    label: 'ATK',
                    data: atkData,
                    borderColor: "brown",
                    backgroundColor: "brown",
                    fill: false
                }
            ]
        },
        options: {
            tooltips: {
                callbacks: {
                    label: function(tooltipItem, data) {
                        return "Level: " + tooltipItem.xLabel + ", " + data.datasets[tooltipItem.datasetIndex].label + ": " + tooltipItem.yLabel;
                    }
                }
            },
            title: {
                display: false,
            },
            scales: {
                xAxes: [{
                    stacked: false,
                    ticks: {
                        interval: 20
                    }
                }],
                yAxes: [{
                    stacked: false,
                    ticks: {
                        min: 0,
                        max: 25000,
                        stepSize: 5000,
                    }
                }],
            }
        }
    };
    var myLineChart = new Chart(ctx, config);
    document.getElementById("legend").style.display = "";
}

function goToAddServant() {
    var servantName = encodeURI(decodeHtml("Amor (Caren)"));
    var url = "https://gamepress.gg/grandorder/node/add/user_servant?edit[title]=" + servantName + "&edit[field_servant]=" + servantName + " (939096)";
    window.location.href = url;
}

function decodeHtml(html) {
    var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
    txt.innerHTML = html;
    return txt.value;
}

<div class="field field--name-field-read-more field--type-link field--label-hidden field__item"><a href="https://community.gamepress.gg/c/fate-grand-order" class="button">Read More</a></div>

<span class="gp-tier-modal">
<div id="gp-tier-modal" class="modal">

<div class="modal-content-gp-tier" id="modal-cont-gp-tier">
<span class="remove" onclick="closeModalGP()"><i class="fa fa-times-circle" aria-hidden="true"></i></span>
<div id="unit-expl-gp"></div>
</div>
</div>
</span>
<script>
  var gpLoaded = false;
    $(document).ready(function() {
          bindButtons();
      });

    function bindButtons(){
      var showButtons = document.getElementsByClassName("show-expl");
          for(var i = 0; i < showButtons.length; i++){
            showButtons[i].onclick = showModalGP;
          }
    }

    function showModalGP(e){
      document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "0";
      var modal = document.getElementById('gp-tier-modal');
      if(!modal){
        return;
      }
      var content = $(e.target).data('content');
      var title = $(e.target).data('title');
      var titleID = title.replace(":", "");
      let nid = $(e.target).data("nid");
      if(nid){
        titleID = nid;
      }
      var explDiv = document.getElementById(titleID + "-expl-container");
      var text = decodeHtml(explDiv.innerHTML);
      title = "<div class='expl-title'>" + title + "<\/div>"
      var modal2 = document.getElementById("unit-expl-gp");
      modal2.innerHTML = title + text;
      modal.style.display = "block";
      gpLoaded = false;
    }

    function closeModalGP(){
      var modal = document.getElementById('gp-tier-modal');
      if(!modal){
        return;
      }
      modal.style.display = "none";
      gpLoaded = true;
      document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "";
    }
    $('body').click(function (e) {
        if(typeof(isDBL) == 'undefined'){
          var id = e.target.id;
        var parents = document.getElementById("modal-cont-gp-tier");
        var modal = document.getElementById("gp-tier-modal");
        if(!modal){
          return;
        }
        if(modal.style.display == "block" && gpLoaded && !(parents.contains(e.target))){
          modal.style.display = "none";
          document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "";
          gpLoaded = false;
        }
        else{
          gpLoaded = true;
        }
      }
      function decodeHtml(html) {
        var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
        txt.innerHTML = html;
        return txt.value;
    }

  });
</script>
